UML Conventions Comformance Report

[ 27/06/2020 ]

Publications Office of the European Union
Luxembourg
https://op.europa.eu

Table of contents

Constrain type

Abstract

eProcurement UML model needs to conform to a set of UML conventions described elsewhere. A conformance checking script was developed to execute tests to the UML model and generate errors or warnings when encountered.

This document was automatically generated by the conformance checking script and comprises the UML conformance violations.

The organisation of this document is based on major types of UML elements and connectors that are employed in the eProcurement conceptual model. They are as follows: Classes, Enumerations, Datatypes, Packages, Associations, Dependencies and Generalisations. Each major section lists model items that need correction of errors or consideration of warnings.

The UML model in file ePO-CM-v2.0.1-2020-06-27-mappings.eap.xmi was tested at 17:18 on June 27, 2020.

Unmet class conventions
The class dct:Agent has no attributes provided. A class should define some attributes.
dct:Agent is missing a description. All concepts should be defined or described.

Unmet class conventions

dt:Text
The attribute name dt:Text is invalid. The attribute name must start with a lower case.
The attribute type Text is deprecated. Attributes should use XSD or RDF datatypes. The suggested alternative for Text is rdf:langString
The attribute dt:Text type Text is not defined in the model. Every used type should be defined. This applies to The standard datatypes (e.g XSD or RDF), which should be re-declared in the model and serving as proxies.
The name dt:Text is not unique. The Concept names should be unique within the model; while the relations may repeat but should not overlap with concept names.
dt:Text is missing a description. All concepts should be defined or described.
